#### Azorult
POST retrieve method, unique pattern with lot's of '/' and ')'
~~~

User-Agent: Mozilla/4.0 (compatible; MSIE 6.0b; Windows NT 5.1)
Host: 51.38.76.57
Content-Length: 103
Cache-Control: no-cache

J/.8/.:/.</.?/.>O.(8.I/.>/.9/.>K.>8.N/.I/.;/.</.;N.>:.NL.?N.>8.(9.L/.8/.</.4/.4/.I/.?/.>H.(9.(9.(9.(9.I
